<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палата.html>пала́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">paláta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палата.html>пала́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палата.html>пала́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палата.html>пала́т</a></b>)

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родильный.html>роди́льная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палата.html>пала́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rodílʹnaja paláta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">labour ward, obstetrics ward, maternity ward</span></div></dd>

</ul></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палата.html>пала́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paláta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Often ascribed to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">раlа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sword</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ач</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ač</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">*раlаcı</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sword bearer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***палец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>палец</a> (259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пальць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">palĭcĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*palьcь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thumb, finger</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pálec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>finger or toe
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pálec nogí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">toe</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bolʹšój pálec</i> ― <span class="e-translation">thumb; big toe</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указательный.html>указа́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ukazátelʹnyj pálec</i> ― <span class="e-translation">forefinger, index finger</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">srédnij pálec</i> ― <span class="e-translation">middle finger</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:безымянный.html>безымя́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bezymjánnyj pálec</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ring finger</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мизинец.html>мизи́нец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mizínec</i> ― <span class="e-translation">little finger, little toe</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предохранительный.html>предохрани́тельный</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:резиновый.html>рези́новый</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">predoxranítelʹnyj (rezínovyj) <b>pálec</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">finger stall</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рить</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pálec</b> o <b>pálec</b> ne udáritʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to lift a finger</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шевельнуть.html>шевельну́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pálʹcem</b> ne ševelʹnútʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to lift a finger</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льца</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рота.html>рот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:класть.html>клади́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>pálʹca</b> v rot ne kladí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is not to be trifled with (watch your step with him)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозь.html>сквозь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">smotrétʹ skvozʹ <b>pálʹcy</b> na štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to look through one’s fingers at something; to wink at something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обвести.html>обвести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вокруг.html>вокру́г</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льца</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obvestí vokrúg <b>pálʹca</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cheat, to dupe, to deceive, to take in</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тронуть.html>тро́нет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>pálʹcem</b> nikovó ne trónet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he wouldn’t hurt a fly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высосать.html>вы́сосать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льца</a></b> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výsosatʹ iz <b>pálʹca</b> štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fabricate something; to dream the whole thing up</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцев</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">znatʹ štó-libo kak svoí pjatʹ <b>pálʹcev</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have something at one’s fingertips; to know something backwards and forwards, to know something like the back of one’s hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">popástʹ <b>pálʹcem</b> v nébo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be wide of the mark</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показывать.html>пока́зывать</a> <i>or</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:указывать.html>ука́зывать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <i>+ acc.</i></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pokázyvatʹ <i>or</i> ukázyvatʹ <b>pálʹcem</b> na <i>+ acc.</i></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to point one’s finger at</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцев</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">znatʹ kak svoí pjatʹ <b>pálʹcev</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have at one’s fingertips</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>ко́сти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцев</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kósti <b>pálʹcev</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">finger bones</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>ко́сти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцев</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ног</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kósti <b>pálʹcev</b> nog</i> ― <span class="e-translation">toe bones</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>technical</i>) (crank) pin, finger, cam</li></ol>

***палить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a> (8018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*paliti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">palítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to singe
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опалить.html>опали́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to destroy with fire, to scorch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустановленный.html>неустано́вленные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>ли́ца</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>паля́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Neustanóvlennyje líca <b>palját</b> domá.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Unidentified persons are <b>burning</b> houses.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спалить.html>спали́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">spalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to burn (a bonfire, lantern, etc.; for the purposes of lighting)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scorch, to be very hot <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the sun, the day, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to torment <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of feelings, experiences</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fire, to shoot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>Там</a> где́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиди́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снайпер.html>сна́йпер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tam gdé-to sidít snájper i <b>palít</b> po nam.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There's a sniper sitting somewhere there and <b>firing</b> at us.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to talk very quickly
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпалить.html>вы́палить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výpalitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">transitive: to burn</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жечь.html>жечь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сжигать.html>сжига́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sžigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">palítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спалить.html>спали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch (someone) doing something illegal or disallowed, to catch red-handed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предок.html>пре́дки</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ли</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неоднократно.html>неоднокра́тно</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Menjá prédki <b>palíli</b>, i neodnokrátno.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My parents caught me and on multiple occasions.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:паломничество.html>пало́мничество</a> (26423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паломник.html>пало́мник</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">palómnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ество</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-estvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***палубный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:палубный.html>па́лубный</a> (31051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палуба.html>па́луба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">páluba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палубный.html>па́лубный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pálubnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deck
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:палубный.html>па́лубные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>до́ски</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pálubnyje</b> dóski</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>deck</b> planking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> decked <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having a deck</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:палубный.html>па́лубная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яхта.html>я́хта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pálubnaja</b> jáxta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a <b>decked</b> yacht</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> carrier; carrier-based <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">capable of taking off from and landing on an aircraft carrier</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:палубный.html>па́лубный</a></b> торпедоно́сец</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pálubnyj</b> torpedonósec</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>carrier</b> torpedo bomber</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пальнуть.html>пальну́ть</a> (19769)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">palítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***памятовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:памятовать.html>па́мятовать</a> (21743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pámjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:памятовать.html>па́мятовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pámjatovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember, to recall</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This verb is no longer used much except in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:памятовать.html>па́мятуя</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> ...</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pámjatuja, o ...</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">recalling ...</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опа́мятоваться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opámjatovatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pamętь</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>пан</a> (4930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">pan</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>пан</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pan</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>па́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>паны́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>па́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>пано́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>па́нов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пани.html>па́ни</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">па́нский</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sometimes  derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Polish landowner, feudal lord, or gentleman
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>пан</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>пропа́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pan</b> íli propál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">all or nothing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">title  or  form of address</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sir, mister, gentleman, lord (usually in Polish, Czech, Slovak, Ukrainian or sometimes Belarusian contexts)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sometimes  derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Polack, a Polish person</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In Soviet propaganda, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>пан</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pan</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the sense of a Polish landowner was often used as a derogatory slur but was commonly known for use in modern Poland.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">па́нский</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pánskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пани.html>па́ни</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">páni</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">па́нна</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pánna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:панель.html>пане́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">panɛ́lʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:панель.html>пане́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:панель.html>пане́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:панель.html>пане́лей</a></b>)
